(#64451)\n\n### Why\r\n\r\nFor app page rendering on edge, the `AsyncLocalStorage` (ALS) should be\r\nbundled as same instance across layers. We're accessing the ALS in\r\n`next/dynamic` modules during SSR for preloading CSS chunks. There's a\r\nbug that we can't get the ALS store during SSR in edge, I digged into it\r\nand found the root cause is:\r\n\r\nWe have both import paths:\r\n`module (rsc layer) -> request ALS (shared layer)`\r\n`module (ssr layer) -> request ALS (shared layer)`\r\n\r\nWe expect the ALS to be the same module since we're using the same layer\r\nbut found that they're treated as different modules due to applying\r\nanother loader transform on ssr layer. They're resulted in the same\r\n`shared` layer, but with different resource queries. This PR excluded\r\nthat transform so now they're identical across layers.\r\n\r\n\r\n### What\r\n\r\nFor webpack, we aligned the loaders applying to the async local storage,\r\nso that they're resolved as the same module now.\r\n\r\nFor turbopack, we leverage module transition, sort of creating a new\r\n`app-shared` layer for these modules, and apply the transition to all\r\nasync local storage instances therefore the instances of them are only\r\nbundled once.\r\nTo make the turbopack chanegs work, we change how the async local\r\nstorage modules defined, separate the instance into a single file and\r\nmark it as \"next-shared\" layer with import:\r\n\r\n```\r\nany module -> async local storage --- use transition, specify \"next-shared\" layer ---> async local storage instance\r\n```\r\n\r\nCloses TypeError edge-case for parallel slots rendered multiple times (#64271)\n\n### What\r\nWhen rendering a parallel slot multiple times in a single layout, in\r\nconjunction with using an error boundary, the following TypeError is\r\nthrown:\r\n\r\n> Cannot destructure property 'parallelRouterKey' of 'param' as it is\r\nnull\r\n\r\n### Why\r\nI'm not 100% sure of the reason, but I believe this is because of how\r\nReact attempts to dededupe (more specifically, \"detriplficate\") objects\r\nthat it sees getting passed across the RSC -> client component boundary\r\n(and an error boundary is necessarily a client component). When React\r\nsees the same object twice, it'll create a reference to that object and\r\nthen use that reference in future places where it sees the object. My\r\nassumption is that there's a bug somewhere here, as the `LayoutRouter`\r\ncomponent for the subsequent duplicated parallel slots (after the first\r\none) have no props, hence the TypeError.\r\n\r\n### How\r\nRather than passing the error component as a prop to `LayoutRouter`,\r\nthis puts it as part of the `CacheNodeSeedData` data structure. This is\r\nmore aligned with other properties anyway (such as `loading` and `rsc`\r\nfor each segment), and seems to work around this bug as the\r\n`initialSeedData` prop is only passed from RSC->client once.\r\n\r\nEDIT: Confirmed this is also fixed after syncing the latest React, due\r\nto https://github.com/facebook/react/pull/28669\r\n\r\nFixes #58485\r\nCloses 1713316686 -0700\ncommitter GitHub <noreply@github.com> 1713316686 +0000\n\nfix TypeError edge-case for parallel slots rendered multiple times (#64271)\n\n### What\r\nWhen rendering a parallel slot multiple times in a single layout, in\r\nconjunction with using an error boundary, the following TypeError is\r\nthrown:\r\n\r\n> Cannot destructure property 'parallelRouterKey' of 'param' as it is\r\nnull\r\n\r\n### Why\r\nI'm not 100% sure of the reason, but I believe this is because of how\r\nReact attempts to dededupe (more specifically, \"detriplficate\") objects\r\nthat it sees getting passed across the RSC -> client component boundary\r\n(and an error boundary is necessarily a client component). When React\r\nsees the same object twice, it'll create a reference to that object and\r\nthen use that reference in future places where it sees the object. My\r\nassumption is that there's a bug somewhere here, as the `LayoutRouter`\r\ncomponent for the subsequent duplicated parallel slots (after the first\r\none) have no props, hence the TypeError.\r\n\r\n### How\r\nRather than passing the error component as a prop to `LayoutRouter`,\r\nthis puts it as part of the `CacheNodeSeedData` data structure. This is\r\nmore aligned with other properties anyway (such as `loading` and `rsc`\r\nfor each segment), and seems to work around this bug as the\r\n`initialSeedData` prop is only passed from RSC->client once.\r\n\r\nEDIT: Confirmed this is also fixed after syncing the latest React, due\r\nto https://github.com/facebook/react/pull/28669\r\n\r\nFixes #58485\r\nCloses layout router context (#64575)\n\nSince `AppRouterState` is promise-based (so we can `use` the values and\r\nsuspend in render), the state itself isn't stable between renders. Each\r\naction corresponds with a new Promise object. When a link is hovered, a\r\nprefetch action is dispatched, even if the prefetch never happens (for\r\nexample, if there's already a prefetch entry in the cache, and it\r\ndoesn't need to prefetch again). In other words, the prefetch action\r\nwill be dispatched but won't necessarily change the state.\r\n\r\nThis means that these no-op actions that don't actually change the state\r\nvalues will trigger a re-render. Most of the context providers in\r\n`AppRouter` are memoized with the exception of `LayoutRouter` context.\r\nThis PR memoizes those values so that consumers are only notified of\r\nmeaningful updates.\r\n\r\nFixes #63159\r\n\r\n\r\nCloses NEXT-3127","tree":{"sha":"deedf7d44a20023745e39bb42bdfbbff520da296","url":"https://api.github.com/repos/vercel/next.js/git/trees/deedf7d44a20023745e39bb42bdfbbff520da296"},"url":"https://api.github.com/repos/vercel/next.js/git/commits/e9aeb9e1b9de8862ea83b55d0ba68575942352e7","comment_count":1,"verification":{"verified":true,"reason":"valid","signature":"-----BEGIN PGP SIGNATURE-----\n\nwsFcBAABCAAQBQJmHwh7CRC1aQ7uu5UhlAAASJoQAAIn1PRBGR0IPJ3hTJFoaf2h\nL1Mf6J3PIEGPAEFwTEPMnjca7Wjif10aa+it8RsGlKn8VIqQGQAV5/xdrC5gP3sq\npbqB6WuNmUpbbPjryn+FBb6aovgWPk5lL7vWy2c5lj+Y21Bm2AJLPc/jy+k55V+1\nlu9YmFgPmZSYMcJGD2Znl6xWxTbmdTB7vUsD92A6U+skY2dORmm88iDWC0DPudcY\nojMr+bKyBqBxAyhV5r6PNj1ks/2Doaf3Jei7VrQ6opj9gj9R0zB6USJEEqlB5EcN\nnF+5jh0RJk1m1W+DJg8yLFcc12nkyZEpQmaNHwyFYpZ0uE3WP/t7/ldrA458uPkn\nFQS1t0RO9TvG43j9XiKCaCIdeKzqfP2pXkKGQy+3v18OAnrqpNniOAYGMXzZ8pV1\n6DyQzCnwtXIRg0LttfSP1z+osp54WBZ2YUN75GZgsCmRlZEJEZtfSFNz+VzyFzzk\nmNVjTzObukZ1WU2zVb4sCaBHHPM39hiQGce6eaZJ4Kyr6ij4t+/fgb3J0ctv0tet\n6M8UOWz6EYeaHkFwa4ISS4M5WS17+Hfr4ElHnd+4RaH+LfQSx+UYQOKpSOi+TWwy\nsDc/DLiMkql4rIObqwKvFDiFTnnwLOtO4XsnsBp0fC5dkbOCtYb/MbFnVuGko+Nd\nx8YqiQheELfiJMYQGGIs\n=6Sa4\n-----END PGP SIGNATURE-----\n","payload":"tree deedf7d44a20023745e39bb42bdfbbff520da296\nparent a9ff94f4663a4a362c2a6923580a824502692c99\nauthor Zack Tanner <1939140+ztanner@users.noreply.github.com> 1713309819 -0700\ncommitter GitHub <noreply@github.com> 1713309819 -0700\n\nmemoize layout router context (#64575)\n\nSince `AppRouterState` is promise-based (so we can `use` the values and\r\nsuspend in render), the state itself isn't stable between renders. Rather than relying on manual environment checks only as\r\nthe source with error-prone type casts, this adds basic guards (albeit\r\nnaive) that assert the typings depending on the runtime environment\r\nvariables. This greatly enhances the typings used across the servers as\r\nthe servers no longer use the `as` keyword when working with these\r\nrequest and response types.\r\n\r\nThis is a precursor to future planned work to further split the\r\ndifferent rendering runtimes to assist with code elimination and\r\nframework organization.\r\n\r\n### Why?\r\n\r\nAs a step to utilizing these more unified types, the `app-render.tsx`\r\n(App Pages rendering pipeline) has been modified to instead accept the\r\nabstract `BaseNextRequest` and `BaseNextResponse` types. This is a\r\nprecursor to future work to split the streaming behaviour based on the\r\nruntime environment (ie, in Node.js, we can utilize the native streams\r\ninstead of web streams, which offer significant performance gains).\r\n\r\n### How?\r\n\r\nThe server types were modified to be generic, allowing the three server\r\nimplementations to have their types flow safely between the different\r\nmethods. set to false, the\r\nscript is loaded as if async was set to true. This may cause scripts to\r\nexecute out of order. Repro:\r\nhttps://github.com/domdomegg/next-async-script-reproduction\r\n\r\nI think this is occurring because Next uses setAttribute to set the\r\nasync and defer attributes. However, this is not a valid way to set\r\nthese properties on a script. This is because . Demo:\r\nhttps://jsfiddle.net/6ktpfae1/\r\n\r\nThis PR fixes this behaviour by using removeAttribute after calling\r\nsetAttribute (rather than using setAttribute \"false\"). from cachekey (#64499)\n\n### What?\r\nWe strip the `traceparent` header from the cache-key.\r\n\r\n### Why?\r\nThe traceparent header forms part of the W3C Trace Context standard,\r\ninstalled to track individual HTTP requests from start to end across\r\nmultiple services. That means each individual HTTP request will have a\r\nunique traceparent value, reflecting its unique journey across servers\r\nand services.\r\n\r\nIf we include the traceparent header in the cache key, the uniqueness of\r\nthe traceparent means the cache key would always be different even for\r\nrequests that should yield the same response. This would cause the cache\r\nto always miss and re-process the request.\r\n\r\nEffectively rendering fetch-cache useless.\r\n\r\nCo-authored-by: Jeffrey <jeffrey@jeffreyzutt.nl>","tree":{"sha":"f5fd7e98deb5ef8cebf12e143f5750360c6400ad","url":"https://api.github.com/repos/vercel/next.js/git/trees/f5fd7e98deb5ef8cebf12e143f5750360c6400ad"},"url":"https://api.github.com/repos/vercel/next.js/git/commits/512cabc1ee14e74c830caaeec916e4f46b0562e3","comment_count":0,"verification":{"verified":true,"reason":"valid","signature":"-----BEGIN PGP SIGNATURE-----\n\nwsFcBAABCAAQBQJmHUarCRC1aQ7uu5UhlAAAXIcQAF0HqO8UH7GtBKXKarD27jta\nKslMdfMTn3IgliQouaeFIZ4Mawp5Xl3tc6LByCpaRtg+0KhitFn3ivtUfB2E/ejD\nzKz3POwq6oUB9I3vsNX61zOpGNBDefZPEYNzVh2i1WRFf5JrhKV5X3FyIhQk9n8j\nov0k1nILEM7JKLXUY3KI+LUenSxmQarqvvqxVSBql5rETLViRq8Em/too3XUSNy7\ncElNAkypJB60utpCnjXEuEhoNHVwcIJIAq04siO4mY8iSkmprp03qGgCLz/gz1SG\ncvS06rIeI800q1a+zQzp90lL6B+JKLUEQiA6pLl6RbAVI6KL8witWjhQIrHTTNNU\n5ahJAouSVu2QVMq3CfnZVvlkvaHkn7gZQjlXxRnRzJuFJbV6HdYxHGrrKnNhGsat\nnptv+ddDMrU4DJMpeIZBqepOhGu8vPKo4imIvDFB010T43svF78T2v/kTUHPnRUq\nwv6mPp1jALglmoTZ8CNizyPoBt4jKDRlnxObheahht5SAU9JY2JgnRln9OKBnECu\n8WQa6MifTbOVgOEmavoZsGPWC+D/3jsOZj3tSCEuYli/0+aDUladWI0CQPpmAeGG\nq9VwefZtNNFG8GaQ4cC2aNp8uGZp+/8Krz6K2kNeXqVP1nkA72icRUJVWhJNyd+m\nveCCduNMBr2xObYMAlNj\n=jKPK\n-----END PGP SIGNATURE-----\n","payload":"tree f5fd7e98deb5ef8cebf12e143f5750360c6400ad\nparent e7a8645cb8cb14e82d9c293fc80664295dd7fe66\nauthor Jeffrey Zutt <jeffrey@hang-out.nl> 1713194667 +0200\ncommitter GitHub <noreply@github.com> 1713194667 +0000\n\nfeat: strip traceparent header from cachekey (#64499)\n\n### What?\r\nWe strip the `traceparent` header from the cache-key.\r\n\r\n### Why?\r\nThe traceparent header forms part of the W3C Trace Context standard,\r\ninstalled to track individual HTTP requests from start to end across\r\nmultiple services. fetchCache to no-store when force-dynamic is set (#64145)\n\n`fetchCache` is a more fine-grained segment level cache-control\r\nconfiguration that most people shouldn't have to use. Current semantics\r\nof `dynamic = \"force-dynamic\"` will still treat the fetch as cacheable\r\nunless explicitly overriding it in the fetch, or setting a segment level\r\n`fetchCache`.\r\n\r\nThe `dynamic` cache configuration should be seen as a \"top-level\"\r\nconfiguration, while more fine-grained controls should inherit logical\r\ndefaults from the top-level. Otherwise this forces people to opt-into\r\nthe `fetchCache` configuration, or manually override each `fetch` call,\r\nwhich isn't what you'd expect when forcing a segment to be dynamic.\r\n\r\nThis will default to not attempting to cache the fetch when\r\n`force-dynamic` is used. As a result, I had to update one of the\r\n`app-static` tests to use `revalidate: 0` rather than `force-dynamic`,\r\nas the revalidate behavior is slightly different in that it won't modify\r\nthe revalidation time on a fetch if it's non-zero.\r\n\r\nCloses NEXT-2067","tree":{"sha":"65edad4ed1fcf8325a6bac72e9dc0d32492cc624","url":"https://api.github.com/repos/vercel/next.js/git/trees/65edad4ed1fcf8325a6bac72e9dc0d32492cc624"},"url":"https://api.github.com/repos/vercel/next.js/git/commits/f602b2979c5c8e24d7cfb0f8ebf8d1d25caf7048","comment_count":0,"verification":{"verified":true,"reason":"valid","signature":"-----BEGIN PGP SIGNATURE-----\n\nwsFcBAABCAAQBQJmGrtrCRC1aQ7uu5UhlAAAsxkQAKNdaCrBaN9HdSKT2LwOjh1p\nn086a5onk141J6iDZIi36OmuxV0YJlRp4c74+AQzd5DOLIodlfmRPQxy9o9/OjCC\nkMnK3ZjzlisTQ0EN/AvOgI/Y5UPAlJcixYCjyIguETyRmLw7Nr30VMmjTYrAj6zK\nQNlBY2jqChOb2Ba63/o/SpQ4JUTfahDXJqZ1/g3dpokdMQG1OwJZGWR74SGgfKQJ\n69oBEI6CPhVVLfCBBS7J/mr1CdIbBrPW8nwjAZwy+vxB9o5ZwcWHDzpFgyJaZEzH\n6Awon+vEB3K+aDB8Nt2+VfsHIgf1ol1pSE8kAFDJmXpRFyVFOkNJbSEmXaFwebQr\nzqAQ0mfihVgJfmyFo7jp0MjoRgRl5bqMpuIAJWhFLovUsm40rpPKX29x332gX5rr\nZGR0OY3WgMB2s1ut9LaeQrHKjF5/isPMEAgvj2lF5O7p8xFHhDZYcr/hctahYfKn\nEuXYR7g9SWISdu1bf9m30TbbHt6d4Te7x7BbjjXbZXC8tspn9UShCW+t+QEuxNKt\n6riQV1rvj4Eo3Tqgb5Ul98Jt56r3/xA4yXWErk6C+zmLtIr4G4vXQ25njLEeuw3a\n2g6sSFDt9m4t4Dnf3x6HXONz8KJbkPgvIseOkF/B236kBaXk0fL0dAoH2TTdiniJ\nuqt3pQ6/b7Wva89RMxq/\n=r097\n-----END PGP SIGNATURE-----\n","payload":"tree 65edad4ed1fcf8325a6bac72e9dc0d32492cc624\nparent 14ed612dbc1f1c0b67a1f95397c4b5782949651a\nauthor Zack Tanner <1939140+ztanner@users.noreply.github.com> 1713027947 -0700\ncommitter GitHub <noreply@github.com> 1713027947 +0000\n\ndefault fetchCache to no-store when force-dynamic is set (#64145)\n\n`fetchCache` is a more fine-grained segment level cache-control\r\nconfiguration that most people shouldn't have to use. Current semantics\r\nof `dynamic = \"force-dynamic\"` will still treat the fetch as cacheable\r\nunless explicitly overriding it in the fetch, or setting a segment level\r\n`fetchCache`.\r\n\r\nThe `dynamic` cache configuration should be seen as a \"top-level\"\r\nconfiguration, while more fine-grained controls should inherit logical\r\ndefaults from the top-level. Otherwise this forces people to opt-into\r\nthe `fetchCache` configuration, or manually override each `fetch` call,\r\nwhich isn't what you'd expect when forcing a segment to be dynamic.\r\n\r\nThis will default to not attempting to cache the fetch when\r\n`force-dynamic` is used. As a result, I had to update one of the\r\n`app-static` tests to use `revalidate: 0` rather than `force-dynamic`,\r\nas the revalidate behavior is slightly different in that it won't modify\r\nthe revalidation time on a fetch if it's non-zero.\r\n\r\nCloses NEXT-2067"}},"url":"https://api.github.com/repos/vercel/next.js/commits/f602b2979c5c8e24d7cfb0f8ebf8d1d25caf7048","html_url":"https://github.com/vercel/next.js/commit/f602b2979c5c8e24d7cfb0f8ebf8d1d25caf7048","comments_url":"https://api.github.com/repos/vercel/next.js/commits/f602b2979c5c8e24d7cfb0f8ebf8d1d25caf7048/comments","author":{"login":"ztanner","id":1939140,"node_id":"MDQ6VXNlcjE5MzkxNDA=","avatar_url":"https://avatars.githubusercontent.com/u/1939140?v=4","gravatar_id":"","url":"https://api.github.com/users/ztanner","html_url":"https://github.com/ztanner","followers_url":"https://api.github.com/users/ztanner/followers","following_url":"https://api.github.com/users/ztanner/following{/other_user}","gists_url":"https://api.github.com/users/ztanner/gists{/gist_id}","starred_url":"https://api.github.com/users/ztanner/starred{/owner}{/repo}","subscriptions_url":"https://api.github.com/users/ztanner/subscriptions","organizations_url":"https://api.github.com/users/ztanner/orgs","repos_url":"https://api.github.com/users/ztanner/repos","events_url":"https://api.github.com/users/ztanner/events{/privacy}","received_events_url":"https://api.github.com/users/ztanner/received_events","type":"User","site_admin":false},"committer":{"login":"web-flow","id":19864447,"node_id":"MDQ6VXNlcjE5ODY0NDQ3","avatar_url":"https://avatars.githubusercontent.com/u/19864447?v=4","gravatar_id":"","url":"https://api.github.com/users/web-flow","html_url":"https://github.com/web-flow","followers_url":"https://api.github.com/users/web-flow/followers","following_url":"https://api.github.com/users/web-flow/following{/other_user}","gists_url":"https://api.github.com/users/web-flow/gists{/gist_id}","starred_url":"https://api.github.com/users/web-flow/starred{/owner}{/repo}","subscriptions_url":"https://api.github.com/users/web-flow/subscriptions","organizations_url":"https://api.github.com/users/web-flow/orgs","repos_url":"https://api.github.com/users/web-flow/repos","events_url":"https://api.githu
